### 1.2 Design Metaphor: "Mission Control"

AgentWorld's UI adopts a **Mission Control** metaphorâ€”users are operators observing and guiding a living simulation. Like NASA's mission control:

- **Central viewport** shows the "mission" (simulation) status
- **Peripheral panels** provide telemetry (metrics, logs, memory states)
- **Control surfaces** allow intervention without disrupting flow
- **Timeline** enables rewinding and replaying any moment

### 1.3 Visual Language

| Element | Treatment | Rationale |
|---------|-----------|-----------|
| Agents | Colored avatars with trait-derived hues | Quick personality recognition |
| Topology | Force-directed graph with animated edges | Show communication flow |
| Memory | Layered cards with importance gradients | Visualize memory salience |
| Time | Horizontal timeline with step markers | Scrub through simulation |
| Metrics | Sparklines and gauges | Glanceable health indicators |

---

### 2.2 Usage Frequency Matrix

| Flow | Dr. Maya | Alex | Sam | Jordan |
|------|----------|------|-----|--------|
| Create simulation | Weekly | Daily | Daily | Daily |
| Design personas | Monthly | Weekly | Daily | Weekly |
| Configure topology | Daily | Rarely | Rarely | Daily |
| Run focus group | Rarely | Daily | Never | Rarely |
| Generate data | Sometimes | Never | Daily | Sometimes |
| Analyze results | Daily | Daily | Weekly | Daily |
| A/B testing | Daily | Weekly | Sometimes | Daily |
| Debug/inspect | Sometimes | Never | Sometimes | Daily |

---

### 4.2 Mode Switching

Users can seamlessly switch between interfaces:

- **Web â†’ CLI**: "Copy as CLI command" button on any action
- **CLI â†’ Web**: `agentworld open :id` opens simulation in browser
- **Real-time sync**: Changes in CLI immediately visible in Web UI

---

## 10. Accessibility & Responsive Design

## Document History

| Version | Date | Author | Changes |
|---------|------|--------|---------|
| 1.1.0 | Jan 2025 | - | Added: Border radius, shadows, icons, theme stance (Appendix C); Data visualization specs (Appendix D); Empty/loading/first-run states (Appendix E); Roles & permissions (Appendix F). Fixed: TraitSlider canonical direction rule (left=0.0/low, right=1.0/high) |
| 1.0.0 | Jan 2025 | - | Initial specification |

---

*This specification provides a comprehensive blueprint for AgentWorld's user interface. Implementation should proceed iteratively, starting with core flows (simulation creation, live monitoring) before expanding to advanced features (A/B testing, analytics).*
